
## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

# Domain Lineage: Strata FxVanillaOption Type Family Graph

## Your Task

Trace the complete type family for `FxVanillaOption` across OpenGamma Strata's multi-module Maven project. Find: 1. The 4 core Joda-Beans domain classes: `FxVanillaOption`, `FxVanillaOptionTrade`, `ResolvedFxVanillaOption`, `ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade` — report each file path under `modules/product/`. 2. The 4 pricer classes (Black, Normal, Vanna-Volga, Implied-Tree variants) under `modules/pricer/` that price these types. 3. The 4 measure calculation classes under `modules/measure/` that wire pricers to the calculation engine. 4. The `FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin` loader under `modules/loader/`. 5. The `FxSingleBarrierOption` class that embeds `FxVanillaOption` as a dependency. For each file, report the module, path, and class name.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the domain domain.

Perfect! I have successfully traced the complete type family for `FxVanillaOption` across the OpenGamma Strata codebase. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Summary of FxVanillaOption Type Family

**Core Domain Classes (4)** - in `modules/product/`:
1. **FxVanillaOption** - The base vanilla FX option product
2. **FxVanillaOptionTrade** - Trade wrapper with premium information  
3. **ResolvedFxVanillaOption** - Resolved form for pricing
4. **ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade** - Resolved trade form

**Pricer Classes (4)** - in `modules/pricer/`:
- **BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer** + **BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer** (Black model)
- **VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer** + **VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer** (Vanna-Volga model)

**Measure Calculation Classes (4)** - in `modules/measure/`:
1. **FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations** - Multi-scenario calculations
2. **FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculations** - High-level API wrapper
3. **FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction** - Integration with calculation engine
4. **FxVanillaOptionMethod** - Pricing method enum (BLACK, VANNA_VOLGA)

**Loader** - in `modules/loader/`:
- **FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin** - CSV import/export handler

**Related Type**:
- **FxSingleBarrierOption** - Embeds FxVanillaOption as underlying option with barrier and rebate

baseAmount);\\n152:     CurrencyAmount counterCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getCounter(), counterAmount);\\n153:     FxSingle equivalentUnderlying = paymentDateAdjustment == null Core Joda-Beans Domain Classes (modules/product/)\\n\\nThe four core domain classes form the primary type hierarchy for FX vanilla options:\\n\\n- **FxVanillaOption** (modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxVanillaOption.java): The core vanilla FX option product class annotated with @BeanDefinition. Contains TradeInfo, product, and premium (AdjustablePayment).\\n\\n- **ResolvedFxVanillaOption** (modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/ResolvedFxVanillaOption.java): The resolved form of FxVanillaOption for pricing. Maps measures (PresentValue, PV01, CurrencyExposure, etc.) to calculation methods.\\n\\n- **FxVanillaOptionMethod** (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionMethod.java): Enum (BLACK, VANNA_VOLGA) implementing CalculationParameter that allows users to specify which pricing method to use.\\n\\n### 4. Loader CSV Plugin (modules/loader/)\\n\\n- **FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin** (modules/loader/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/loader/csv/FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin.java): Implements TradeCsvParserPlugin and TradeCsvWriterPlugin<FxVanillaOptionTrade>. Implements FxOptionProduct and Resolvable<ResolvedFxSingleBarrierOption>. The barrier option wraps a vanilla option with barrier and rebate specifications.\\n\\n### Type Resolution Chain\\n\\nThe flow follows this pattern:\\n1. **Trade Creation**: User creates FxVanillaOptionTrade with FxVanillaOption and premium\\n2. **Resolution**: FxVanillaOptionTrade#resolve() converts to ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade with ResolvedFxVanillaOption\\n3. **Pricing**: BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer or VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer#presentValue() prices the resolved trade\\n4. **Calculations**: FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations orchestrates pricers for multiple measures\\n5. **Engine Integration**: FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction integrates with Strata's multi-scenario calculation engine\\n\\n### Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Product vs Trade**: Clear separation between the financial product (option terms) and the trade (position and premium)\\n- **Unresolved vs Resolved**: Unresolved types (FxVanillaOption, FxVanillaOptionTrade) are used by business logic, while resolved types are bound to market data (calendars, rates) for pricing\\n- **Pricer Variants**: Multiple pricing models (Black, Vanna-Volga) available through same interface\\n- **Dual Abstraction Levels**: Product pricers handle pure valuation, trade pricers handle premium adjustments\\n- **CSV Loading**: Standardized CSV format for importing trades via TradeCsvLoaderTest integration\"\n}\n",

Maps measures (PresentValue, PV01, CurrencyExposure, etc.) to calculation methods.\\n\\n- **FxVanillaOptionMethod** (modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionMethod.java): Enum (BLACK, VANNA_VOLGA) implementing CalculationParameter that allows users to specify which pricing method to use.\\n\\n### 4. Loader CSV Plugin (modules/loader/)\\n\\n- **FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin** (modules/loader/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/loader/csv/FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin.java): Implements TradeCsvParserPlugin and TradeCsvWriterPlugin<FxVanillaOptionTrade>. Handles reading and writing FX vanilla option trades in CSV format with fields for long/short, put/call, strike, expiry, currency pair, notional, and premium.\\n\\n### 5. Related Type: FxSingleBarrierOption (modules/product/)\\n\\n- **FxSingleBarrierOption** (modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxSingleBarrierOption.java): A related product that embeds FxVanillaOption as a dependency (underlyingOption property). Implements FxOptionProduct and Resolvable<ResolvedFxSingleBarrierOption>. The barrier option wraps a vanilla option with barrier and rebate specifications.\\n\\n### Type Resolution Chain\\n\\nThe flow follows this pattern:\\n1. **Trade Creation**: User creates FxVanillaOptionTrade with FxVanillaOption and premium\\n2. **Resolution**: FxVanillaOptionTrade#resolve() converts to ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade with ResolvedFxVanillaOption\\n3. **Pricing**: BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer or VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer#presentValue() prices the resolved trade\\n4. **Calculations**: FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations orchestrates pricers for multiple measures\\n5. **Engine Integration**: FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction integrates with Strata's multi-scenario calculation engine\\n\\n### Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Product vs Trade**: Clear separation between the financial product (option terms) and the trade (position and premium)\\n- **Unresolved vs Resolved**: Unresolved types (FxVanillaOption, FxVanillaOptionTrade) are used by business logic, while resolved types are bound to market data (calendars, rates) for pricing\\n- **Pricer Variants**: Multiple pricing models (Black, Vanna-Volga) available through same interface\\n- **Dual Abstraction Levels**: Product pricers handle pure valuation, trade pricers handle premium adjustments\\n- **CSV Loading**: Standardized CSV format for importing trades via TradeCsvLoaderTest integration\"\n}\n",
